<UserId.>117253256529424057889<//UserId.><username>Zane Gregorian</username>< Date>
1616950374869<//Date>
<Rate>5< /Rate>< review>
Great experience! The staff was incredibly friendly and helpful, they gave a great tour of the menu including specials and substitutions for vegetarians in our party.

The food itself was excellent; they say the mole is cooked for three days and it shows! Incredible depth of flavor, the kind of place you want to scrape every drop of sauce with leftover chips.

I usually don‚Äôt prefer corn tortillas even though it‚Äôs more traditional, but the fresh, hand-made ones here are absolutely to die for.

Finally their drink menu was really varied and interesting. Seems like everything they offer pairs well. I got the Santa Iguana, which was very refreshing and vegetal, and complemented the rich and earthy mole.

The only difficulty is of course seating. There are currently Covid restrictions, so not a fault of the restaurant. To their credit, they have a lovely outdoor patio with great atmosphere and music. I made a reservation in the morning day-of, but I saw people turned away at the door who tried to walk up and get seated on a weekend night. Just make a reservation and you should be fine!

Overall, highly recommend!</review>

We heard of San Diego Kabob Shack from the Eastlake to go Facebook group. We were planning in visiting earlier but for one reason or another it didn't happen until  8/6/2021. We ordered a chicken kabob plate and  a falafel wrap plus a couple of unsweetened iced teas. The food was very tasty specifically the chicken kabob. My wife loved the falafel wrap. Service was a little bit on the slow end but we understand that they might be understaffed - No big deal. To go packaging was excellent specifically for people like us that eat our food in our car. <GmapID>0x80d94dab151ac567:0x70877709ce54a6b</GmapID><Text>I was lucky enough to stumble into San Diego Kabob Shack today when looking for a place to eat with my clients.

Chula Vista has a shortage of "STAND OUT" Middle Eastern food but SDKS is a beacon of flavor in a desert.

We ordered the garlic hummus, the Triple Kabob Kombo, the Gyro Wrap, and the Zaatar Fries.

The garlic hummus is very light on the garlic but enough to give you the proper balance of sesame, garlic, and chickpea. And it's super creamy and amazing to spread on the fresh hot pita bread.

The Gyro Wrap came on toasted pita, a bed of veggies, a HEAP of Gyro Meat, and their amazing housemaid tzatziki sauce.

The kabob is extremely tender and cooked to perfection. I don't know how they get the beef so tender!! And the chicken has the perfect balance of onion, lemon, and garlic!

Finally, my personal favorite was the zaatar fries which were skinny fries, extra fried for the crunch, seasoned with zaatar.

I asked for all 4 sauces to try with the fries and my personal favorite was the green chutney.

I recommend eating here and trying out a new thing every time. I'm going back for the koobideh burger!!

This is a new, family owned business, who's trying. Leave a glowing review, tip heavy, and call them to cater your next event!!</Text>< Pics>

We heard of San Diego Kabob Shack from the Eastlake to go Facebook group. We were planning in visiting earlier but for one reason or another it didn't happen until  8/6/2021. We ordered a chicken kabob plate and  a falafel wrap plus a couple of unsweetened iced teas. The food was very tasty specifically the chicken kabob. My wife loved the falafel wrap. Service was a little bit on the slow end but we understand that they might be understaffed - No big deal. To go packaging was excellent specifically for people like us that eat our food in our car. <Text>I was lucky enough to stumble into San Diego Kabob Shack today when looking for a place to eat with my clients.

Chula Vista has a shortage of "STAND OUT" Middle Eastern food but SDKS is a beacon of flavor in a desert.

We ordered the garlic hummus, the Triple Kabob Kombo, the Gyro Wrap, and the Zaatar Fries.

The garlic hummus is very light on the garlic but enough to give you the proper balance of sesame, garlic, and chickpea. And it's super creamy and amazing to spread on the fresh hot pita bread.

The Gyro Wrap came on toasted pita, a bed of veggies, a HEAP of Gyro Meat, and their amazing housemaid tzatziki sauce.

The kabob is extremely tender and cooked to perfection. I don't know how they get the beef so tender!! And the chicken has the perfect balance of onion, lemon, and garlic!

Finally, my personal favorite was the zaatar fries which were skinny fries, extra fried for the crunch, seasoned with zaatar.

I asked for all 4 sauces to try with the fries and my personal favorite was the green chutney.

I recommend eating here and trying out a new thing every time. I'm going back for the koobideh burger!!

This is a new, family owned business, who's trying. Leave a glowing review, tip heavy, and call them to cater your next event!!<//Text><user>118370279121964396584<//user></record></dataset><record>

<Review>My Cuban husband and I went to El Cubano today and we really loved it. The atmosphere is welcoming and friendly. The staff was so pleasant and accommodating that you just felt comfortable right away. My husband and I dug into our usual favorites of Masitas de Puerco ( fried pork ) and Lechon Asado ( roast pork ) which is soaked in a Cuban marinade known as Mojo. Both meals were served with  Congri, Black Beans,  White Rice and Sweet Plaintains.  As a side we had Yuca and of course the fresh bread. All the while we were consistently being checked on and drinks refreshed. Sadly they are still waiting for a liquor license, but that‚Äôs expected. When we waited for a day that would have been decent with crowd and availability,  you expect a certain type of customer service with a smaller attendance.

On first impression the  esthetic is pleasing and offers a select seating selection from a fire pit to "a" large group table (yes be aware of group size if you consider this place). But the appeal was over run with the plants in the seating path that could be a trip Hazzard later.

After meeting the host,  even with minimal attendance,  she seemed flustered and discombobulated. She stated it would be 35 minutes for a party of 2. After counting tables filled to empty tables and how many wait staff were skulking about.  The ratio was completely viable to be seated immediately,  but we waited,  almost an hour.

The seating request was was completely denied and even with ensuing rain,  we were seated at an uncovered fire pit.

Very unsatisfied I asked for the names and checked the menu for the prices.  In fact the prices were absurd for the serving size and quality of the lack luster grab bag costco quality food.

Overall,  this entire situation was unpleasant and not only would I not suggest to an every day crowd,  I suggest an experienced wait staff,  host,  and a deep evaluation of your meals and prices to accurately fit what you're attempting to reach and not bulking prices to attempt and meet the actual high end eateries just along this road.< /Review>< pictures>

The wine list was vast with emphasis on their signature Small Barn varietals & wine by the bottle (by the glass is available on select wines). I would hope for ‚Äúby the glass‚Äù people their may be more red wines available in e future.
